$(function() {
CURRENCY_CONF.language = 'en_US';
CURRENCY_CONF.usd_cny = Number('6.485499999999999' || 6.3);
Big.DP = 40;

function bindAddressSearch() {
var $container = $('.global-search-form-container');
$('#input-address').on('input', updateAddressSearch);
$container.find('.currency-list-menu a').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
var currency = $(this).text();
var urlName = $(this).data('urlname');
$('#addressSearchForm button[type="submit"]').prop('disabled', $('#input-address').val() === '');
$('#currency-toggle .btn').text(currency);
$('#input-currency').val(urlName.toUpperCase());
});
$container.find('.icon-clear-search').on('click', function() {
$('#input-address').val('');
$(this).hide();
updateAddressSearch();
});
}
// click outside to close dropdown
function bindDropdownClose() {
$(document).on('click touchstart', function (e) {
var $toggle = $('.footer-pop, .btn-app-download-ios, .btn-app-download-android');
if (!$toggle.is(e.target) && $toggle.has(e.target).length === 0 && $('.popover').has(e.target).length === 0) {
(($toggle.popover('hide').data('bs.popover')||{}).inState||{}).click = false;
}
});
}
function bindNavbarCollapse() {
$('.page-wrapper > .header .navbar-collapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function(e) {
$(this).parents('.header').addClass('collapse-show');
}).on('hidden.bs.collapse', function(e) {
$(this).parents('.header').removeClass('collapse-show');
updateHeaderClass();
});
}
function updateHeaderTheme() {
var $headerIn = $('.layout-header-in');
var $header = $('header.header');
if ($headerIn.length > 0) {
$(window).on('scroll', function() {
if ($header.hasClass('collapse-show')) return;
updateHeaderClass();
});
}
}
function updateHeaderClass() {
var $headerIn = $('.layout-header-in');
var $header = $('header.header');
if ($(document).scrollTop() >= $headerIn.innerHeight() - ($(window).width() > 991 ? ($('.page-index').length > 0 ? 120 : 10) : 0)) {
if (!$header.hasClass('header-white')) {
$header.addClass('header-white header-fix-top animate');
$header.trigger('header.fixtop.on');
}
} else {
if ($header.hasClass('header-white') && !$header.hasClass('header-no-banner')) {
$header.removeClass('header-white header-fix-top animate');
$header.trigger('header.fixtop.off');
}
}
}
function updateAddressSearch() {
var currencyArr = [], urlName, displayCode;
var regxArr = {"bch": "(q[a-zA-Z0-9]{27,60}|[13][a-zA-Z0-9]{27,34})", "bsv": "(q[a-zA-Z0-9]{27,60}|[13][a-zA-Z0-9]{27,34})", "etc": "(?:0[Xx])?[0-9A-Fa-f]{40}", "eth-address": "(0[xX])?[0-9A-Fa-f]{40}", "zec": "t[13][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{33}|zc[1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{93}", "zen": "z[nst][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{33}|zc[1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{93}", "sc": "[0-9A-Fa-f]{76}", "dash": "[7X][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xmr": "[48][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{94,105}(?:\\.[0-9a-fA-F]{16,64})?", "dcr": "D[1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xzc": "[Za][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "rvc": "[Rr][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{33}", "hns": "hs1[qpzry9x8gf2tvdw0s3jn54khce6mua7l]{39,59}", "kda": "[0-9a-z]{64}", "chi": "C[a-zA-Z0-9]{27,35}", "ckb": "ck[0-9a-zA-Z]+", "sero": "[123456789ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijkmnopqrstuvwxyz]{44,}", "bcd": "[13][a-zA-Z0-9]{27,34}", "beam": "[0-9a-fA-F]{40,90}", "hc": "H[1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "dgb-sha256d": "[DS][0-9A-Za-z]{27,35}", "dgb-scrypt": "[DS][0-9A-Za-z]{27,35}", "dgb-skein": "[DS][0-9A-Za-z]{27,35}", "dgb-qubit": "[DS][0-9A-Za-z]{27,35}", "dgb-odocrypt": "[DS][0-9A-Za-z]{27,35}", "mona": "[MP][0-9a-zA-Z]{20,60}", "btm": "bm1[qpzry9x8gf2tvdw0s3jn54khce6mua7l]+", "xvg-blake2s": "[DE][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xvg-scrypt": "[DE][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xvg-x17": "[DE][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xvg-lyra": "[DE][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "xvg-groestl": "[DE][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{27,35}", "pgn": "P[a-zA-Z0-9]{27,34}", "rvn": "[Rr][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{33}", "rvn-pri": "[Rr][1-9A-HJ-NP-Za-km-z]{33}"};
var $container = $('.global-search-form-container');
var $btnCurrencyToggle = $("#currency-toggle .btn");
var $inputAddress = $('#input-address');
var $inputCurrency = $('#input-currency');
var $btnSearchSubmit = $('#addressSearchForm button[type="submit"]');
var $listMenu = $container.find('.currency-list-menu');
var $btnClearSearch = $container.find('.icon-clear-search');
var txt = $inputAddress.val().replace(/\s/g, '');
$inputAddress.val(txt);
if (!txt) {
$btnCurrencyToggle.text('Currency');
$btnSearchSubmit.prop('disabled', true);
$btnClearSearch.hide();
$listMenu.find('.currency-item').show();
return;
} else {
$btnClearSearch.show();
}
Object.keys(regxArr).forEach(function(key) {
if (RegExp('^' + regxArr[key] + '$').test(txt)) {
var $item = $('.currency-list-menu .' + key);
currencyArr.push(key);
urlName = $item.data('urlname');
displayCode = $item.data('displayCode');
}
});
if (currencyArr.length == 1) {
$btnCurrencyToggle.text(displayCode);
$btnSearchSubmit.prop('disabled', false);
$inputCurrency.val(urlName && urlName.toUpperCase() || '');
$listMenu.removeClass('show');
} else if (currencyArr.length > 1) {
$btnCurrencyToggle.text('Currency');
$btnSearchSubmit.prop('disabled', true);
$container.find('.currency-list-menu .currency-item').filter(function() {
var isMatch = $.inArray($(this).data('key'), currencyArr) > -1;
if (isMatch) $(this).show();
return !isMatch;
}).hide();
$listMenu.addClass('show');
} else if (txt) {
$btnCurrencyToggle.text('Currency');
$btnSearchSubmit.prop('disabled', true);
$container.find('.currency-list-menu .currency-item').show();
$listMenu.addClass('show');
}
}
// change language
function bindChangeLanguage() {
$('.change-lang').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
Cookies.remove('lang');
Cookies.set('lang', $(this).data('lang'), {domain: ".f2pool.com"});
location.reload();
});
}
// footer popover
function bindFooter() {
if ($(window).width() > 991) {
$('.footer-pop').each(function() {
$(this).popover({
html: true,
trigger: 'hover click',
placement: 'top',
container: $(this),
template: '<div class="popover footer-popover"><div class="popover-body"></div></div>',
content: function() {
return $(this).find('.footer-pop-content').prop('outerHTML');
}
}).on('show.bs.popover', function() {
$(this).addClass('active');
}).on('hide.bs.popover', function() {
$(this).removeClass('active');
});
});
} else {
var $modal = $('#globalFooterModal');
$('.footer-pop').on('click', function() {
$modal.find('.container').html($(this).find('.footer-pop-content').clone().css('display', 'block'));
$modal.modal({ show: true });
});
}
}
function setCalculator () {
var $calcModal = $('#modalGlobalCalculator');
var $iptProfit = $calcModal.find('.input-profit');
var $iptHashrate = $calcModal.find('.input-hashrate');
var calcMode = 'hash-to-profit';
var minerData;
var config;
$calcModal.on('show.bs.modal', function(e) {
var $target = $(e.relatedTarget);
config = $target.data('config');
initCalcModal();
}).on('hide.bs.modal', function() {
$('#calcSetupCollapse').collapse('hide');
});
// change currency
$calcModal.find('.dropdown-currency .dropdown-item').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
config = $(this).data('config');
initCalcModal();
});
// hashrate input event
$iptHashrate.on('change', function() {
if (calcMode === 'profit-to-hash') return;
var profit = getResult(config, $(this).val(), 'toProfit');
$iptProfit.val(profit);
toFiatMoney(profit);
});
// profit input event
$iptProfit.on('change', function() {
if (calcMode === 'hash-to-profit') return;
var hash = getResult(config, $(this).val(), 'toHashrate');
$iptHashrate.val(hash);
toFiatMoney($(this).val());
});
// convert button click event
$calcModal.find('.convert').on('click', function() {
var oldMode = calcMode;
var $in = $calcModal.find('.container-in');
var $out = $calcModal.find('.container-out');
var $title1 = $calcModal.find('.container-dropdown .calc-title');
var $title2 = $out.find('.calc-title');
var temp = $title1.text();
if (calcMode === 'hash-to-profit') {
calcMode = 'profit-to-hash';
} else {
calcMode = 'hash-to-profit';
}
$in.append($out.find('.calc-input'));
$out.append($in.find('.calc-input').eq(0));
$in.find('input').prop('disabled', false);
$out.find('input').prop('disabled', true);
$title1.text($title2.text());
$title2.text(temp);
$calcModal.removeClass(oldMode).addClass(calcMode);
});
// collapse toggle
$('#calcSetupCollapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function() {
var currency = $(this).parents('.section-calculator').find('.dropdown-toggle .currency-name').text();
$('.modal-global-calculator .btn-collapse').html('<i class="far fa-angle-up"></i> Minimize');
}).on('hide.bs.collapse', function() {
$('.modal-global-calculator .btn-collapse').html('<i class="far fa-angle-down"></i> More Settings');
});
// setup
$calcModal.find('.setup .form-control, .miner-table .ipt-elec').on('change', function() {
var res;
var $iptHashrate = $calcModal.find('.input-hashrate');
var $iptProfit= $calcModal.find('.input-profit');
updateCalcMiners(config);
if ($calcModal.find('.container-in .input-hashrate')) {
res = getResultfromCustomConf(config, $iptHashrate.val(), 'toProfit');
$iptProfit.val(res);
} else {
res = getResultfromCustomConf(config, $iptProfit.val(), 'toHashrate');
$iptHashrate.val(res);
}
toFiatMoney($iptProfit.val());
});
$calcModal.find('.miner-table').on('change', '.ipt-miner-price', function() {
var $row = $(this).parents('tr');
var minerId = $row.data('id');
var rowId = $row.attr('id');
var data;
if (minerId && minerData) {
data = minerData.find(function(item) {
return item.id === minerId;
});
if (data) {
$(this).data('usd', CURRENCY_FUNC.toUSD($(this).val()));
$row.replaceWith(getSingleMinerTpl(data, config));
CURRENCY_FUNC.updateMoney($('#' + rowId), 'formatPriceWithoutSeparator');
}
}
});
function initCalcModal() {
var currency = config.currency;
var display_currency_code = config.display_currency_code;
var $btnToggle = $calcModal.find('.dropdown-currency .dropdown-toggle');
var $toggleImg = $btnToggle.find('img');
var $setupCollapse = $calcModal.find('.setup-collapse');
var imgName = (currency === 'eth-address') ? currency : currency.split('-')[0];
var profit;
// unit profit without rate
config.unitProfit = Big(config.estimatedProfit).div(CURRENCY_CONF.scales[config.scale || 1]).div((100 - (config.rate || 0)) / 100).toFixed();
if (currency === 'btc') {
var ppsUnitProfit = Big(1).div(config.difficulty).times(6.25 * 86400 / Math.pow(2, 32)).toFixed();
config.gasFee = (Big(config.unitProfit).div(ppsUnitProfit).minus(1)).times(100).toFixed();
}
$iptHashrate.val(1);
if (currency === 'xch') {
$calcModal.find('.hashrate-unit').text(config.scale + config.unit);
} else {
$calcModal.find('.hashrate-unit').text(config.scale + config.unit + '/s');
}
$calcModal.find('.profit-append').text(display_currency_code.split('-')[0] + '/day');
$toggleImg.attr('src', $toggleImg.data('s').replace('{}', imgName));
$btnToggle.find('.currency-name').text(display_currency_code);
// add linker to advanced calculator for btc
if(currency!=='btc'){
$calcModal.find('.link-advanced-calc').addClass("d-none").removeClass("d-flex align-items-center")
}else{
$calcModal.find('.link-advanced-calc').removeClass("d-none").addClass("d-flex align-items-center")
}
if (currency === 'btc' || currency === 'eth') {
$calcModal.find('.comment-pps').hide();
$calcModal.find('.comment-pps-plus').show();
} else {
$calcModal.find('.comment-pps').show();
$calcModal.find('.comment-pps-plus').hide();
}
//难度
$setupCollapse.find('.setup-difficulty').toggle(config.currency === 'btc').find('.form-control').val(config.difficulty);
if (!config.price) config.price = 0;
//币价
$setupCollapse.find('.setup-price .form-control').val(parseFloat(config.price.toFixed(2))).data('usd', config.price);
//费率
$setupCollapse.find('.setup-rate .form-control').val(config.rate);
updateCalcMiners(config);
profit = getResult(config, 1, 'toProfit');
//收益
$iptProfit.val(profit);
CURRENCY_FUNC.updateMoney($calcModal);
toFiatMoney(profit);
}
function updateCalcMiners(config) {
var $calcContainer = $('#modalGlobalCalculator');
var $minerTable = $calcContainer.find('.miner-table');
if ($minerTable.data('currency') === config.currency && minerData) {
updateTable(minerData);
} else {
$.post({
url: '/miners/bycoin',
data: {
currency_code: config.currency.split('-')[0],
limit: 5
}
}, function(res) {
var data = res.data;
minerData = res.data;
$minerTable.data('currency', config.currency);
updateTable(data);
}).fail(function() {
$('.miner-table-container').hide();
});
}
}
function updateTable(data) {
var tpl = [];
var $calcContainer = $('#modalGlobalCalculator');
var $minerTable = $calcContainer.find('.miner-table');
if ($.isArray(data) && data.length > 0) {
data.forEach(function(item) {
tpl.push(getSingleMinerTpl(item, config));
});
$('.miner-table-container').show();
$minerTable.find('tbody').html(tpl.join(''));
} else {
$('.miner-table-container').hide();
}
CURRENCY_FUNC.updateMoney($minerTable.find('tbody'), 'formatPriceWithoutSeparator');
}
}
function getResult(config, val, type) {
var ret, temp;
var scale = CURRENCY_CONF.scales[config.scale || 1];
var customConf = getCustomVal();
var base = Big(config.unitProfit).times(scale).times((100 - (customConf.rate || 0)) / 100);
val = Number(val);
if (isNaN(val) || val <= 0 || !config.unitProfit) {
ret = '';
} else {
temp = (config.price + '').split('.')[1];
ret = type === 'toProfit' ? Big(val).times(base) : Big(val).div(base);
ret = ret.toFixed(ret.gte(1e6) ? 2 : (ret.gte(100) ? 4 : 8));
}
return ret;
}
function getResultfromCustomConf(config, val, type) {
var customConf = getCustomVal();
var unitProfit;
var estimatedProfit;
if (config.currency === 'btc') {
if (customConf.difficulty && customConf.price_usd && customConf.rate) {
unitProfit = Big(1).div(customConf.difficulty).times(6.25 * 86400 / Math.pow(2, 32)).times(Big(1).plus(Big(config.gasFee).div(100))).toFixed();
} else {
unitProfit = Big(config.estimatedProfit).div(CURRENCY_CONF.scales[config.scale || 1]).div((100 - (config.rate || 0)) / 100).toFixed()
}
}
if (unitProfit) config.unitProfit = unitProfit;
return getResult(config, val, type);
}
function toFiatMoney(val) {
var $toFiatMoney = $('.to-fiat-money');
var coinPrice = getCustomVal().price_usd;
var fiat = Big(val || 0).times(coinPrice);
$toFiatMoney.find('.money-val').data('usd', fiat).text(Big(CURRENCY_FUNC.exchange(fiat.toFixed())).toFixed(2));
}
// by USD
function getSingleMinerTpl(minerData, coinConfig) {
var temp = [];
var rowId = 'miner-' + minerData.id + '-' + coinConfig.currency;
var $row = $('#' + rowId);
var minerPrice, mixedCoinData, mixedMinerData, profitData;
var customConf = getCustomVal();
mixedCoinData = $.extend({}, coinConfig, {
rate: customConf.rate,
price: customConf.price_usd,
difficulty: customConf.difficulty
});
if ($row.length) {
minerPrice = $row.find('.ipt-miner-price').data('usd') || 0;
mixedMinerData = $.extend({}, minerData, { price: isNaN(minerPrice) ? 0 : minerPrice });
} else {
mixedMinerData = $.extend({}, minerData, { price: minerData.price < 0 ? 1000 : minerData.price });
}
profitData = computeProfit(mixedCoinData, mixedMinerData, customConf.elecFee_usd);
temp.push(minerData.name,
CURRENCY_FUNC.formatHashrate(minerData.hashrate),
minerData.power + '<span class="unit unit-right">W</span>',
'<span class="money-symbol unit unit-left">$</span><span class="money-val" data-usd="' + profitData.revenue_24h + '"></span>',
'<span class="money-symbol unit unit-left">$</span><span class="money-val" data-usd="' + profitData.elec_24h + '"></span>',
'<span class="money-symbol unit unit-left">$</span><input class="money-val ipt-miner-price form-control" data-usd="' + mixedMinerData.price + '" value="" />',
profitData.recoupDays >= 0 ? profitData.recoupDays : ('<span class="text-danger">Expected to not ROI</span>'));
return '<tr id="' + rowId+ '" data-id="' + minerData.id + '"><td>' + temp.join('</td><td>') + '</td></tr>';
}
function getCustomVal() {
var $calcContainer = $('#modalGlobalCalculator');
return {
price_usd: CURRENCY_FUNC.toUSD($calcContainer.find('.setup-price .form-control').val() || 0),
rate: $calcContainer.find('.setup-rate .form-control').val() || 0,
difficulty: $calcContainer.find('.setup-difficulty .form-control').val(),
elecFee_usd: CURRENCY_FUNC.toUSD($calcContainer.find('.ipt-elec').val() || 0),
};
}
// by USD
function computeProfit(coinData, minerData, elecFee) {
var coins_24h, revenue_24h, elec_24h, profit_24h, recoupDays;
if (minerData.hashrate) {
if (coinData.currency === 'btc' && coinData.difficulty && minerData.hashrate) {
coins_24h = Big(minerData.hashrate).div(coinData.difficulty).times(6.25 * 86400 / Math.pow(2, 32));
} else if (coinData.currency !== 'btc' && coinData.unitProfit && minerData.hashrate) {
coins_24h = Big(coinData.unitProfit).times(minerData.hashrate);
}
}
if (coinData.rate > 0) coins_24h = coins_24h.times((100 - coinData.rate) / 100);
if (coins_24h && coinData.price) revenue_24h = coins_24h.times(coinData.price);
if (minerData.power) elec_24h = Big(minerData.power).times(elecFee || 0).times(0.024);
if (revenue_24h && elec_24h) profit_24h = revenue_24h.minus(elec_24h);
if (profit_24h && minerData.price) {
recoupDays = profit_24h <= 0 ? -1 : Big(minerData.price).div(profit_24h);
}
return {
currency: coinData.currency,
coins_24h: coins_24h && coins_24h.toFixed(8),
revenue_24h: revenue_24h && revenue_24h.toFixed(8),
elec_24h: elec_24h && elec_24h.toFixed(8),
profit_24h: profit_24h && profit_24h.toFixed(8),
recoupDays: recoupDays && Math.ceil(recoupDays.toString()),
};
}
function bindScrollToTop() {
var $window = $(window);
var $doc = $(document);
var $btn = $('.btn-global-to-top');
if ($doc.scrollTop() > 50) $btn.addClass('animate');
$btn.on('click', function() {
window.scroll({ top: 0, left: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
});
$window.on('scroll', function() {
var scrollTop = $doc.scrollTop();
if (!$btn.hasClass('animate') && scrollTop > 500) {
$btn.addClass('animate');
} else if ($btn.hasClass('animate') && scrollTop < 100) {
$btn.removeClass('animate');
}
});
}
function getMiningUserHashrate() {
var $dropdown = $('.dropdown-global-user-menu');
var $item, data, content, userName, hashData;
$dropdown.on('show.bs.dropdown', function() {
$.post({
url: '/multi-user-hashrate',
data: {
currency_code: 'btc',
}
}, function(res) {
data = res.data && res.data.users;
if (!data) return;
$dropdown.find('.dropdown-menu .dropdown-user').each(function() {
var $item = $(this);
var itemData = data[$item.data('name')];
if (!itemData) {
$item.remove();
return;
}
hashData = (itemData.hashrate || '0.00') + ' ' + $item.data('suffix');
$item.find('.mining-user-hashrate').text(hashData);
$item.toggleClass('zero-hash', !Number(itemData.hashrate));

});
});
});
}
function bindUserSearch() {
var $searchIpt= $('.search-account-input');
var searchKey;
$('.mining-user-section .item-common').each(function(idx) {
$(this).data('index', idx);
});
$searchIpt.on('input', function() {
searchKey = $(this).val();
updateUserMenu(searchKey);
});
}
function updateUserMenu(searchKey) {
var $section = $('.mining-user-section');
var arr = [];
searchKey = searchKey.toLowerCase();
$section.find('.item-search').each(function() {
$(this).removeClass('item-search');
});
$section.find('.dropdown-item-user').sort(function(a, b) {
var $a = $(a);
var $b = $(b);
var idxA = $a.data('index');
var idxB = $b.data('index');
return idxA === idxB ? ($a.hasClass('item-common') ? -1 : 1) : (idxA - idxB);
}).appendTo($section);
if (searchKey !== '') {
$section.find('.item-common').each(function(idx, el) {
var $this = $(this);
if ($this.data('name').toLowerCase().match(searchKey) || ($this.data('desc') && $this.data('desc').toString().toLowerCase().match(searchKey))) {
arr.push($(this).addClass('item-search'));
}
});
$section.prepend(arr);
}
}
function bindInputGroupEffect() {
// focus effect
$('body').on('focus', '.input-group input[type="text"].form-control', function() {
$(this).parents('.input-group').addClass('active');
}).on('blur', '.input-group input[type="text"].form-control', function() {
$(this).parents('.input-group').removeClass('active');
});
}
function bindAutoProtocol() {
var $modalAutoProtocol = $('#modalAutoProtocol');
$modalAutoProtocol.on('click', '.btn-submit', function() {
$.ajax({
type: 'POST',
url: '/user/account/enable-auto-switch',
}).done(function(response, status, xhr) {
if (response.status == "fail") {
$('.status-toast').remove();
$('body').append('<div class="status-toast fail">Submission failed.</div>');
$('.status-toast').delay(5000).hide(0);
} else {

location.href = "/jump?next=%2Fminers&currency=auto-equihash";

}
}).fail(function() {
$('.status-toast').remove();
$('body').append('<div class="status-toast fail">Submission failed.</div>');
$('.status-toast').delay(5000).hide(0);
});
});
$('.dropdown-global-currency .dropdown-item').on('click', function(e) {
if ($(this).hasClass('has-multi-currency')) {
e.preventDefault();
} else {
return;
}
$modalAutoProtocol.modal('show');
});

}

});
}

});

}

$('.search-box-miner input').on('input', function() {
var val = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
var $listItemLeft = $('.list-container-left .list-body > .list-row');
var $listItemRight = $('.list-container-right .list-body > .list-row');
var matchCount = 0;
var searchKey = SEARCH_KEY;
ALL_DATA && ALL_DATA.forEach(function(item, idx) {
var isMatch = searchKey.reduce(function(res, key) {
return res || (item[key].toLowerCase().indexOf(val) > -1);
}, false);
if (isMatch) matchCount++;
$listItemLeft.eq(idx).toggleClass('hide', !isMatch);
$listItemRight.eq(idx).toggleClass('hide', !isMatch);
});
$('.list-container-empty').toggle(searchKey !== '' && matchCount === 0);
});
$('.list-area').on('click', '.list-body .list-row', function(e) {
location.href = '/miner?id=' + $(this).data('id');
});
$(window).on('resize', function() {
CURRENCY_FUNC.updateListHeaderStyle();
updateCurrencySelectContainer();
$table = $('#sort-by-currency-table');
if ($.fn.dataTable.isDataTable($table)){
$table.DataTable().draw(false);
}
});
$('.list-container-right').on('scroll', function() {
$('.list-container-right .list-header').scrollLeft($(this).scrollLeft());
});
function bindMinerTypeNav() {
$('.nav-miner-type').on('click', 'a.nav-link', function(e){
var $this = $(this);
var minerType = $this.data('type')
if( minerType == ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE ){
return;
}
$(window).scrollTop($('.page-top100 .header').outerHeight() - 140);
$('.nav-miner-type').find('.active').removeClass('active');
$this.addClass('active');
if(minerType.startsWith('gpu')) {
$('.list-area').addClass('miner-type-gpu').data('scrollIntoView', false);
$('.nav-miner-type').find('.nav-link.dropdown-toggle').addClass('active').attr('data-type', minerType).text($this.text());
$('.nav-miner-type .dropdown-menu').find('.dropdown-item.active').removeClass('active');
$('.nav-miner-type .dropdown-menu').find('.dropdown-item[data-type="' + minerType +'"]').addClass('active');
} else {
$('.list-area').removeClass('miner-type-gpu').data('scrollIntoView', true);
}
doMinerTypeChange(minerType);
})
$('.nav-miner-type').on('click', 'a.dropdown-item', function(e){
var txt = $(this).text();
var minerType = $(this).data('type');
if( minerType == ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE ){
return;
}
$(window).scrollTop($('.page-top100 .header').outerHeight() - 140);
$(this).siblings().removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active');
$('.nav-miner-type').find('.nav-link.active').removeClass('active');
$('.nav-miner-type').find('.nav-link[data-type="' + minerType +'"]').addClass('active');
$(this).parents('.nav-item').find('.nav-link').attr('data-type', minerType).addClass('active').text(txt);
doMinerTypeChange(minerType);
})
}
function doMinerTypeChange(minerType) {
ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE = minerType;
if (ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'gpu-miner') {
ACTIVE_CURRENCY = 'eth';
} else {
ACTIVE_CURRENCY = 'all';
}
$('.sort-by-miner').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? true : false);
$('.search-box-miner').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? true : false);
$('.sort-by-currency').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? false : true);
$('.search-box-miner-list').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? false : true);
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? true : false);
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').toggleClass('hide', minerType == 'gpu-currency' ? false : true);
initListSortBtn(minerType);
if(minerType == 'gpu-currency') {
getGpuMinerDetail(CHECKED_MINER_ID);
}else{
updateCurrencySelectContainer(COINS_LIST[ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE.startsWith('gpu') ? 'gpu' : ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE], ACTIVE_CURRENCY);
getList();
}
}
function initListSortBtn(minerType) {
if(minerType == 'gpu-currency'){
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').find('.miner').data('id', CHECKED_MINER_ID).text(GPU_MINER_DICT[CHECKED_MINER_ID]);
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').find('.order').data('sort', 'profit_24h').data('type', 'desc').text('Descending by 24h profits');
}else{
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').find('.currency').data('currency', 'all').text('All');
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').find('.order').text('Descending by 24h profits');
}
}
function bindCurrencySelectNav() {
$('.currency-select-container-web').on('click', 'a', function(e){
var currency = $(this).data('currency');
var display_currency_code = $(this).data('display_currency_code');
if(!currency || currency == ACTIVE_CURRENCY) return;
$('.currency-select-container-web').find('a[data-currency="' + ACTIVE_CURRENCY + '"]').removeClass('active');
changeActiveCurrencyPosition(currency, display_currency_code);
$('.currency-select-container-web').find('a[data-currency="' + currency + '"]').addClass('active');
ACTIVE_CURRENCY = currency;
if(ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'gpu-currency') {
var table = $('#sort-by-currency-table').DataTable();
table.column(0).search(currency == 'all' ? '' : currency).draw();
}else {
getList();
}
})
}
function changeActiveCurrencyPosition(currency, display_currency_code){
if ($('.currency-select-container').find('a.item[data-currency="' + currency + '"]').length == 0) {
$('.currency-select-container a.item.custom').remove();
$('.dropdown-miner-list').before('<a class="item custom align-items-center justify-content-center d-flex" data-currency="' + currency + '" data-display_currency_code="'+ display_currency_code +'"' + '>' +
'<img src="https://static.f2pool.com/assets/currencies/logo/' + currency + '-64x64.png" />' +
'<span ' + (currency.length > 5 ? 'style="font-size: 12px;text-align: left;"' : '') + '>' + display_currency_code + '</span></a>');
}
}
function updateCurrencySelectContainer(coins_list, activeCurrency){
if(!coins_list) {
if (ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'gpu-currency') {
coins_list = MINER_COINS_LIST;
} else {
coins_list = COINS_LIST[ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE.startsWith('gpu') ? 'gpu' : ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE];
}
}
if(!activeCurrency) activeCurrency = ACTIVE_CURRENCY;
$container = $('.currency-select-container');
var content = '<a class="item d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center" data-currency="all" data-display_currency_code="all">All</a>';
var dropdownMenu = ''
var display_num;
var win_width = $(window).width()
if (win_width <= 767){
display_num = 999;
}else if( win_width > 767 && win_width <= 991){
display_num = 6;
}else if( win_width > 991 && win_width < 1080){
display_num = 8;
}else if (win_width >= 1080 && win_width < 1200) {
display_num = 10;
}else {
display_num = 12;
}
var len = coins_list.length;
if (len > display_num) {
$container.toggleClass('justify-content-between', true);
dropdownMenu = '<div class="dropdown dropdown-miner-list">' +
'<a class="item d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center item-more dropdown-toggle" ' +
'id="currencySelectDropdown" ' +
'data-toggle="dropdown" ' +
'aria-haspopup="true" ' +
'aria-expanded="false"> ' +
'More <i class="fa fa-chevron-down"></i>' +
'</a>' +
'<div class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-right" aria-labelledby="currencySelectDropdown">'
}else{
$container.toggleClass('justify-content-between', false);
}
coins_list.forEach(function(coin, idx){
var coin_path = '/assets/currencies/logo/' + coin.name + '-64x64.png?ver=' + Math.random();
var display_coin = coin.display_currency_code;
if (idx <= display_num - 1 ){
content += '<a class="item ' + (idx == display_num - 1 ? 'custom' : '') + ' align-items-center justify-content-center d-flex" data-currency="' + coin.name +'" ' + 'data-display_currency_code="' + coin.display_currency_code +'" ' +
(coin.name.length > 5 ? 'style="font-size: 12px;text-align: left;"' : '') + '>' +
'<img src="https://static.f2pool.com'+ coin_path + '" />' + display_coin + '</a>'
}
if (dropdownMenu) {
dropdownMenu += '<a class="dropdown-item" data-currency="' + coin.name +'" data-display_currency_code="' + coin.display_currency_code +'">' +
'<img src="https://static.f2pool.com'+ coin_path + '" />' + display_coin + '</a>'
}
})
if (dropdownMenu) {
content += dropdownMenu + '</div>';
}
content += '</div>'
$container.html(content);
$container.find('a[data-currency="' + activeCurrency + '"]').addClass('active');
}
function initGpuMinerList() {
$.post({
url: '/miners',
data: {
currency_code: '', //means all currency
sort_by: 'hashrate',
sort_type: 'desc',
m_type: 'gpu',
}
}, function(res) {
if (res.data) {
res.data.forEach(function(item, idx){
GPU_MINER_DICT[item.id] = item.name;
if (item.name.startsWith('GTX 1060 8')) {
CHECKED_MINER_ID = item.id;
}
})
$('.search-box-miner-list .checked-miner').text(GPU_MINER_DICT[CHECKED_MINER_ID]).data('id', CHECKED_MINER_ID)
var content = '';
var content1 = '';
for(key in GPU_MINER_DICT) {
content += '<a class="dropdown-item" data-id=' + key + '>' + GPU_MINER_DICT[key] + '</a>';
content1 += '<a class="item" data-id=' + key + '>' + GPU_MINER_DICT[key] + '</a>';
}
$('.search-box-miner-list .dropdown-menu').html(content);
$('.collapse-content.miner-select-container').html(content1);
}
});
}
function bindSearchBoxMinerList() {
$('.search-box-miner-list .dropdown-menu').on('click', 'a', function(e) {
var id = $(this).data('id');
var miner = $(this).text()
if(id == CHECKED_MINER_ID) {
return;
}
$('.search-box-miner-list .dropdown-menu .active').removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active');
$('.search-box-miner-list .checked-miner').text(miner);
CHECKED_MINER_ID = id;
getGpuMinerDetail(id);
})
}
function getGpuMinerDetail(minerId, order) {
$.get({
url: '/miner?id=' + minerId + '&list_page=true',
}, function(res){
var data = res.data.coins;
var minerPower = res.data.power;
MINER_COINS_LIST = [];
var gpuMinerDetailData = [];
if (data) {
for(item in data){
MINER_COINS_LIST.push(data[item]);
if (data[item].hashrate) {
coins_24h = Big(data[item].profit_one_day.toFixed(8));
}
if (coins_24h && data[item].price) revenue_24h = coins_24h.times(data[item].price);
config = {
minerPower: minerPower,
code: item,
display_currency_code: data[item]['display_currency_code'],
coins_24h: coins_24h && coins_24h.toFixed(coins_24h.gte(1e6) ? 2 : (coins_24h.gte(100) ? 4 : 8)),
revenue_24h: revenue_24h && revenue_24h.toFixed(6),
};
gpuMinerDetailData.push($.extend(config, data[item]));
}
}
updateCurrencySelectContainer(MINER_COINS_LIST, ACTIVE_CURRENCY);
fillSortbyCurrencyTable(gpuMinerDetailData, minerId, order);
});
}
function fillSortbyCurrencyTable(data, minerId, order) {
$table = $('#sort-by-currency-table');
if ($.fn.dataTable.isDataTable($table)){
table = $table.DataTable().destroy();
}
if (!data) {
data = [];
}
var order_column = 6; //default order: 'profit_24h'
var order_type = 'desc'; //default order: 'desc'
if (order && order.sort == 'revenue_24h') {
order_column = 4;
order_type = order.type;
}
$table.DataTable({
data: data,
paging: false,
info: false,
dom: "t",
order: [[order_column, order_type]],
autoWidth: false,
scrollX: true,
scrollCollapse: true,
fixedColumns: true,
drawCallback: function(settings) {
var api = this.api();
api.columns([2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]).visible($(window).width() > 767);
},
columns: [{
data: 'code',
className: 'name',
orderable: false,
render: function(data){
var coin_path = '/assets/currencies/logo/' + data + '-64x64.png';
var ret = '<img src="https://static.f2pool.com'+ coin_path + '" />' + data.toUpperCase();
return ret;
}
},{
data: 'hashrate_unit_value',
className: 'hashrate',
orderable: false,
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-';
if($(window).width() > 767){
if (data) {
ret = data + '<span class="unit">' + row.hashrate_unit_str + '</span>'
}
}else {
var symbol = CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$'
if(row.coins_24h) {
ret = row.coins_24h + '<span class="unit">' + row.code.toUpperCase() + '</span>';
}
if(row.revenue_24h) {
ret += ' / ' + '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + row.revenue_24h + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(row.revenue_24h) + '</span>';
}
ret +='<div class="secondary">';
if(row.price) {
ret += '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + row.price + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(row.price) + '</span>';
}
if(row.minerPower){
var elec_24h = Big(row.minerPower).times(ELEC_FEE_USD).times(0.024).toFixed(6);
ret += ' / ' + '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + elec_24h + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(elec_24h) + '</span>';
}
ret +='</div>'
}
return ret;
}
},{
data: 'coins_24h',
className: 'coins-24h',
orderable: false,
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-'
if (data) {
ret = data + '<span class="unit">' + row.code.toUpperCase() + '</span>';
}
return ret;
}
},{
data: 'price',
className: 'price',
orderable: false,
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-'
var symbol = CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$'
if (data) {
ret = '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + data + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(data) + '</span>';
}
return ret;
},
},{
data: 'revenue_24h',
className: 'revenue-24h',
name: 'revenue_24h',
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-'
var symbol = CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$'
if (data) {
ret = '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + data + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(data) + '</span>';
}
return ret;
},
},{
data: 'minerPower',
className: 'elec-24h',
orderable: false,
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-'
var symbol = CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$'
if (data && ELEC_FEE_USD) {
var elec_24h = Big(row.minerPower).times(ELEC_FEE_USD).times(0.024).toFixed(6);
ret = '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + elec_24h + '" data-rule="formatPrice">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice(elec_24h) + '</span>';
}
return ret;
},
},{
data: 'minerPower',
className: 'profit-24h',
name: 'profit_24h',
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '-';
var symbol = CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$';
if (data && ELEC_FEE_USD && row.revenue_24h) {
var elec_24h = Big(row.minerPower).times(ELEC_FEE_USD).times(0.024).toFixed(6);
var profit_24h = Big(row.revenue_24h).minus(elec_24h).toFixed(6)
ret = '<span class="money-symbol">' + symbol + '</span>' +
'<span class="money-val" data-usd="' + profit_24h + '" data-rule="formatPrice_digit">' + CURRENCY_FUNC.formatPrice_digit(profit_24h, 2) + '</span>';;
}
return ret;
},
},{
data: 'code',
className: 'action',
render: function(data, type, row){
var ret = '<a class="btn-calc" href="/calculator?miner_id=' + minerId +'&currency=' + data +'">' +
'Calc' + '</a>';
return ret;
},
}]
})
}
function bindSortbyCurrencyTable() {
$('.sort-by-currency table').on('mouseenter', 'tbody tr', function(e){
$(this).addClass('active')
}).on('mouseleave', 'tbody tr', function(e){
$(this).removeClass('active')
})
}
function getList() {
var sortKey = SORT_KEY;
if (['hashrate', 'power'].indexOf(SORT_KEY) < 0 ||
('' != 'btc' && SORT_KEY != 'coins_24h')) {
sortKey = 'hashrate';
}
$.post({
url: '/miners',
data: {
currency_code: ACTIVE_CURRENCY == 'all' ? '' : ACTIVE_CURRENCY,
sort_by: sortKey,
sort_type: SORT_TYPE || 'desc',
m_type: ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'all' ? '' : (ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE.startsWith('gpu') ? 'gpu' : ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE)
}
}, function(res) {
ALL_DATA = res.data;
fillTable();
});
}
function fillTable() {
var unitPower;
var temp_coins_24h;
if (!ALL_DATA) return;
ALL_DATA.forEach(function(item) {
temp_coins_24h = item.coins_24h;
unitPower = item.hashrate_unit_value ? Big(item.power).div(item.hashrate_unit_value) : Big(0);
item.unit_power = unitPower.toFixed(unitPower.lt(10) ? 1 : 0);
item.revenue_24h = Big(temp_coins_24h).times(item.currency_price).toFixed(6);
item.elec_24h = Big(item.power).times(ELEC_FEE_USD).times(0.024).toFixed(6);
item.profit_24h = Big(item.revenue_24h).minus(item.elec_24h).toFixed(6);
item.elec_rate = Big(item.revenue_24h).eq(0) ? 0 : Big(item.elec_24h).div(item.revenue_24h).toFixed(6);
var temp = Big(temp_coins_24h).toFixed(0).length;
item.coins_24h = Big(temp_coins_24h).toFixed(temp > 6 ? 2 : (temp > 100 ? 4 : 8));
});
if (SORT_KEY) {
if (!SORT_TYPE) SORT_TYPE= 'desc';
ALL_DATA.sort(function(a, b) {
var numA = Number(a[SORT_KEY]);
var numB = Number(b[SORT_KEY]);
numA = isNaN(numA) ? -999999 : numA;
numB = isNaN(numB) ? -999999 : numB;
return (SORT_TYPE === 'desc' ? -1 : 1 ) * (numA - numB);
});
}
$('.list-container .list-body').html('');
$('.list-container-left .list-body').html(template('tpl-list-left', { data: ALL_DATA }));
$('.list-container-right .list-body').html(template('tpl-list', { data: ALL_DATA, symbol: CURRENCY_CONF.globalUnit === 'cny' ? '¥' : '$' }));
if($(window).width() > 767) {
CURRENCY_FUNC.updateListHeaderStyle();
CURRENCY_FUNC.bindStickyHeader($('.page-miner-list .list-container'), 240);
}
}
function initTableSort() {
$('.list-container').on('click', '.col-sort', function() {
if ($(window).width() < 768) return;
var $this = $(this);
var $sortable = $this.find('.sortable');
var sortKey = $sortable.data('sort');
if (!sortKey) return;
SORT_TYPE = $sortable.hasClass('desc') ? 'asc' : 'desc';
SORT_KEY = sortKey;
$('.col-sort .sortable').removeClass('desc asc');
$sortable.addClass(SORT_TYPE);
getList();
});
var $body = $('body');
var $sortContainer = $('.list-sort-container');
$('.list-sort-content').on('show.bs.collapse', function(e) {
if (!$(this).is(e.target)) return;
$body.addClass('modal-open modal-list-sort-open');
if (!$sortContainer.hasClass('fix-top')) {
$sortContainer.addClass('fix-top');
if (!$('header.header').hasClass('header-fix-top')) $(window).scrollTop(0);
}
if ($body.find('.list-backdrop').length === 0) {
$body.append($('<div class="list-backdrop show"></div>'));
} else {
$body.find('.list-backdrop').addClass('show');;
}
initListSortContent();
}).on('hidden.bs.collapse', function(e) {
if (!$(this).is(e.target)) return;
if ($('.list-sort-content.show').length > 0 ||
($('.list-sort-content.collapsing').length > 0 && !$('.list-sort-content.collapsing').is($(this)))) {
return false;
}
$body.removeClass('modal-open modal-list-sort-open');
$body.find('.list-backdrop').remove();;
if (!$('header.header').hasClass('header-fix-top')) $sortContainer.removeClass('fix-top');
});
//点击下拉collapse
$('.list-sort-content .collapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function(){
$(this).prev().find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-down').addClass('fa-chevron-up');
$(this).parents('.list-sort-content').find('.collapse').collapse('hide');
}).on('hide.bs.collapse', function(){
$(this).prev().find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-up').addClass('fa-chevron-down');
})
$('.currency-select-container-h5').on('click', '.item', function(e){
var new_c = $(this).data('currency');
var new_display_c = $(this).data('display_currency_code');
$(this).siblings().removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active');
$('.list-sort-content-miner .btn-currency .info span').text(new_c == 'all' ? 'All' : new_display_c);
$('.list-sort-content-miner .btn-currency').data('currency', new_c);
})
$('.miner-select-container').on('click', '.item', function(e){
var new_miner = $(this).text();
var new_id = $(this).data('id');
$(this).siblings().removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active')
$('.list-sort-content-currency .btn-miner .title').text(new_miner);
$('.list-sort-content-currency .btn-miner').data('id', new_id);
})
$('.order-type-container').on('click', '.item', function(e){
var $container = $(this).parent('.order-type-container');
var new_sort = $(this).data('sort');
var new_type = $(this).data('type');
var content = $(this).text();
$(this).siblings().removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active')
$container.parents('.list-sort-content').find('.btn-sort .title').text(content);
$container.parents('.list-sort-content').find('.btn-sort').data('sort', new_sort).data('type', new_type);
})
$('.list-sort-content .btn-submit').on('click', function(){
var $container = $(this).parents('.list-sort-content')
if (ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'gpu-currency') {
var id = $container.find('.btn-miner').data('id');
var miner = $container.find('.btn-miner .title').text()
var elec = $container.find('.btn-elec .money-val').val();
var sort = $container.find('.btn-sort').data('sort');
var type = $container.find('.btn-sort').data('type');
var sort_content = $container.find('.btn-sort .title').text();
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').find('.miner').text(miner);
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').find('.ipt-elec').val(elec).trigger('change');
$('.list-sort-btn-currency').find('.order').data('sort', sort).data('type', type).text(sort_content);
$container.collapse('hide');
if(id != CHECKED_MINER_ID) {
CHECKED_MINER_ID = id;
getGpuMinerDetail(id, {sort:sort, type: type});
}else {
var column_index = $('#sort-by-currency-table').DataTable().column(sort + ':name').index()
$('#sort-by-currency-table').DataTable().order([column_index, type]).draw();
}
} else {
var currency = $container.find('.btn-currency').data('currency');
var elec = $container.find('.btn-elec .money-val').val();
var sort = $container.find('.btn-sort').data('sort');
var type = $container.find('.btn-sort').data('type');
var sort_content = $container.find('.btn-sort .title').text();
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').find('.currency').text(currency=='all' ? 'All' : currency.toUpperCase());
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').find('.ipt-elec').val(elec).trigger('change');
$('.list-sort-btn-miner').find('.order').text(sort_content);
ACTIVE_CURRENCY = currency;
SORT_KEY = sort;
SORT_TYPE = type;
$container.collapse('hide');
$('.col-sort .sortable').removeClass('desc asc');
$('.list-container .sortable[data-sort="' + sort + '"]').addClass(type);
getList()
}
})
$(document).on('click touchstart', function (e) {
if ($body.hasClass('modal-list-sort-open')) {
var $toggle = $('.list-sort-content');
if (!$toggle.is(e.target) && $toggle.has(e.target).length === 0) {
$toggle.collapse('hide');
}
}
});
}
function initListSortContent() {
if(ACTIVE_MINER_TYPE == 'gpu-currency') {
//init list-sort-content-currency
var $container = $('.list-sort-content-currency');
$container.find('.btn-miner .title').text(GPU_MINER_DICT[CHECKED_MINER_ID]);
$container.find('.btn-miner').data('id', CHECKED_MINER_ID);
$container.find('.miner-select-container .item.active').removeClass('active');
$container.find('.miner-select-container .item[data-id="' + CHECKED_MINER_ID + '"]').addClass('active');
$container.find('.btn-elec input').val($('.list-sort-btn .money-val').val());
$container.find('.order-type-container .item.active').removeClass('active');
var sort = $('.list-sort-btn-currency .order').data('sort');
var type = $('.list-sort-btn-currency .order').data('type');
var text = $container.find('.order-type-container .item[data-sort="'+ sort +'"][data-type="'+ type +'"]').addClass('active').text();
$container.find('.btn-sort .title').text(text);
$container.find('.btn-sort').data('sort', sort).data('type', type);
}else{
//init list-sort-content-miner
var $container = $('.list-sort-content-miner');
$container.find('.btn-currency .info span').text(ACTIVE_CURRENCY == 'all' ? 'All' : ACTIVE_CURRENCY.toUpperCase());
$container.find('.btn-currency').data('currency', ACTIVE_CURRENCY);
updateCurrencySelectContainer();
$container.find('.btn-elec input').val($('.list-sort-btn .money-val').val());
$container.find('.order-type-container .item.active').removeClass('active');
var sort = $('.list-sort-content-miner .order-type-container').find('.item[data-sort="'+ SORT_KEY +'"][data-type="'+ SORT_TYPE +'"]').addClass('active').text();
$container.find('.btn-sort .title').text(sort);
$container.find('.btn-sort').data('sort', SORT_KEY).data('type', SORT_TYPE);
}
}
});
</script>
